RIAA <https://www.riaa.com/>

The Recording Industry Association of America (RIAA) is the trade
organization that supports and promotes the creative and financial
vitality of the major music companies. Its members comprise the most
vibrant record industry in the world, investing in great artists to help
them reach their potential and connect to their fans. RIAA members
create, manufacture, or distribute sound recordings representing
approximately 85% of all legitimate recorded music consumption in the
United States.
